class="grid_wrapper A__TP"></div></div></div><div class="ADS"><div id="taboola-below-home-thumbnails" class="wdt-taboola" data-target_type="mix" data-mode="thumbnails-3x1" data-placement="Below Category Thumbnails" data-pagetype="category" data-ua-type="2" onclick="stpPgtn(event)"></div></div><div class="yizON xEWva"><div class="contentwrapper"><div class="FRAbq  XYnzQ">Check out the <a href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news" target="_blank" title="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/news">latest news</a> in Delhi on The Times of India with a wide range of topics including Delhi’s politics, crime, sports, fashion, culture, civic bodies, <a href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/topics/delhi-traffic-police" target="_blank" title="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/topics/delhi-traffic-police">Delhi traffic</a> and weather updates, new trends, education and civic issues of Delhi. From the regular hustle-bustle of the fast-paced life of the metropolis to the gastronomical delights in Old Delhi. From latest political developments to entertainment-related events or even traffic jams. We cover it all in detail and you can check it all in just one click. Delhi, the capital of India, is also considered the heart of the nation. The massive metropolitan city lies in a triangle formed by the river Yamuna in the east and spurs from the Aravali range in the west and south. The city, a largest and busiest commercial hub in northern India, is also the largest centre of small industries. The IT sector, handloom, fashion, textile and electronic industry contribute a lot to Delhi's economy. The capital has a strong historical background too. It was ruled by some of the most powerful emperors. And thus, it radiates with its syncretic culture. The history of the city is as old as the epic Mahabharata. It was known as Indraprastha, where Pandavas used to live. In due course, eight more cities came alive adjacent to Indraprastha - Lal Kot, Siri, Dinpanah, Quila Rai Pithora, Ferozabad, Jahanpanah, Tughlakabad and Shahjahanabad. The city is divided into two parts - Old Delhi and New Delhi. New Delhi, also called Lutyens' Delhi, bears a striking contrast to Old Delhi with respect to architecture, building materials and layout. However, modern Delhi itself dates back to over a century when the British shifted their capital from Calcutta to Delhi.</div></div></div></div></div><div data-translate-id="cw"><div class="X2plK From latest political developments to entertainment-related events or even traffic jams. We cover it all in detail and you can check it all in just one click. Delhi, the capital of India, is also considered the heart of the nation. The massive metropolitan city lies in a triangle formed by the river Yamuna in the east and spurs from the Aravali range in the west and south. The city, a largest and busiest commercial hub in northern India, is also the largest centre of small industries. The IT sector, handloom, fashion, textile and electronic industry contribute a lot to Delhi's economy. The capital has a strong historical background too. It was ruled by some of the most powerful emperors. And thus, it radiates with its syncretic culture. The history of the city is as old as the epic Mahabharata. It was known as Indraprastha, where Pandavas used to live. In due course, eight more cities came alive adjacent to Indraprastha - Lal Kot, Siri, Dinpanah, Quila Rai Pithora, Ferozabad, Jahanpanah, Tughlakabad and Shahjahanabad. The city is divided into two parts - Old Delhi and New Delhi. New Delhi, also called Lutyens' Delhi, bears a striking contrast to Old Delhi with respect to architecture, building materials and layout. However, modern Delhi itself dates back to over a century when the British shifted their capital from Calcutta to Delhi."},{"tn":"qna_wrapper","name":"DELHI FAQs","id":"faq","items":[{"hl":"DELHI var optOutCookieAge = 365;

function onAcceptOnetrust() {
    setCookieonetrust('optout', '0', window.location.host, 365);
    if (window.localStorage) {
        window.localStorage.setItem('ccpaGdprPopupShown', '1');
    }

}

function onRejectOnetrust() {
    setCookieonetrust('optout', '1', window.location.host, 365);
    if (window.localStorage) {
        window.localStorage.setItem('ccpaGdprPopupShown', '1');
    }
}
var setCookieonetrust = function(name, value, domainName, days) {
    if (!!domainName) {
        var domain = ";domain=" + domainName;
    }
    if (!!days) {
        //Below variable is one day time in mili seconds.
        var _oneDayinMS = 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
        var d = new Date();
        d.setTime(d.getTime() + (days * _oneDayinMS));
        var expires = ";expires=" + d.toUTCString();
    }
    document.cookie = name + "=" + value + ((expires) ? expires : '') + ((domain) ? domain : '') + ";path=/";
}

function attachOnetrustListener() {
    if (window.onetrustEventsAttached) {
        return;
    }
    const onetrustSDK = document.querySelector("#onetrust-consent-sdk");
    if (onetrustSDK) {
        const acceptBtn = onetrustSDK.querySelector("#onetrust-banner-sdk #onetrust-accept-btn-handler");
        const closeBtn = onetrustSDK.querySelector("#onetrust-banner-sdk .onetrust-close-btn-handler");
        const rejectAllBtn = onetrustSDK.querySelector("#onetrust-banner-sdk #onetrust-reject-all-handler");
        // Adding events if acceptBtn is present then related buttons also be presented.
        if (acceptBtn) {
            acceptBtn.addEventListener("click", onAcceptOnetrust);
        }
        if (closeBtn) {
            closeBtn.addEventListener("click", onRejectOnetrust);
        }
        if (rejectAllBtn) {
            rejectAllBtn.addEventListener("click", onRejectOnetrust);
        }
        window.onetrustEventsAttached = true;
        const onetrustPCSDK = onetrustSDK.querySelector("#onetrust-pc-sdk");
        if (!onetrustPCSDK) {
            return;
        }
        const allowBtn = onetrustPCSDK.querySelector("#accept-recommended-btn-handler");
        const rejectBtn = onetrustPCSDK.querySelector(".ot-pc-refuse-all-handler");
        const confirmChoiceBtn = onetrustPCSDK.querySelector(".save-preference-btn-handler");
        // Adding events if allowBtn is present then related buttons also be presented.
        if (allowBtn) {
            allowBtn.addEventListener("click", onAcceptOnetrust);
        }
        if (confirmChoiceBtn) {
            confirmChoiceBtn.addEventListener("click", onAcceptOnetrust);
        }
        if (rejectBtn) {
            rejectBtn.addEventListener("click", onRejectOnetrust);
        }
    }
}

function OptanonWrapper() {
    attachOnetrustListener();

    TimesApps.PopupV2 = function(name, showPopCallback , priority, data) {

      return this.showPopCallback();
    };
  
    TimesApps.PopupV2.prototype.getDetailsPopUp = function() {
      return { ...this };
    };

      this.ready = status;
      if (status === 3) {
        this.setStatus(false);

    TimesApps.PopUpV2Manager = (function() {
      /*
          1. Register overlay
          2. Decide overlay priority
          3. show overlay
  
  
          Register overlay
              - registerOverlay
                  - return onReadyCallback
                  - all popup's call onReadyCallback to mark status, they are ready to be called
              - read priority from config
              - create priority queue
  
          Decide overlay priority
              - read priority queue
              - call if 1st is ready
                      - if status OK  - call
                      - else if not needed to be called, call Next
              -
  
          Show overlay
              - save state in Localstorage
                  - show - true/false
                  - timestamp
  
  
          Config
              - popup list
              - priority for each
              - show frequency
      */
  
      const config = {
        browserStorageKey: 'popUpManagerHigherOrderPopUps',
      };
  
      const constants = {
        HRS_IN_DAY: 24,
        MINS_IN_HR: 60,
        SEC_IN_MIN: 60,
        MilliSEC_IN_SEC: 1000,
      };
  
      const fn = {
        _docReady(forcefully = false) {
          (function() {
            const referrer = document.referrer;
            try {
              if(forcefully) {
                const data1 = JSON.parse(
                  localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
                );
                if (data1.actualData &&
                  Array.isArray(data1.actualData) &&
                  data1.actualData.length > 0 &&
                  (TimesApps.PopUpList[data1.actualData[0].name] &&
                  TimesApps.PopUpList[data1.actualData[0].name].getDetailsPopUp()?.id === 'interstitial')){
                    let pageViewsAfterGDPR = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                    if (!pageViewsAfterGDPR && isNaN(pageViewsAfterGDPR)) {
                        pageViewsAfterGDPR = 0;
                    }
                    localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', pageViewsAfterGDPR + data1.burninterval);
                    return;
                  }
              }
              if (window.localStorage && window.toi_client_side_settings) {
                  if(window.localStorage && localStorage.getItem("ccpaGdprPopupShown") === '1'){
                      let pageViewsAfterGDPR = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                          if (!pageViewsAfterGDPR && isNaN(pageViewsAfterGDPR)) {
                              pageViewsAfterGDPR = 0;
                          }
                          localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', pageViewsAfterGDPR + 1);

                  localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR') &&
                  parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                let data = JSON.parse(
                  localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
                );
                fn._saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews);
                if (
                  data &&
                  Date.now() - data.time >
                  data.burntime * constants.SEC_IN_MIN * constants.MilliSEC_IN_SEC

                  localStorage.removeItem(config.browserStorageKey);
                  localStorage.setItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR', 1);
                  pageViews = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'), 10);
                  data = null;
                }
                if (!data) {
                  window.toi_client_side_settings.time = Date.now();

                  data.actualData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(data.priority));
                  data.actualData.sort((a, b) => a.priority - b.priority);
                  if (!(localStorage.getItem("autoCcpaGdprPopupShown"))){
                    data.nextPageView = 1 + data.burninterval;
                  } else {
                    data.nextPageView = 1;
                  }
                  fn._saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews);
                }
                config.burninterval = data.burninterval;
                config.burntime = data.burntime;
                config.data = data;
                if (config.data.actualData &&
                  Array.isArray(config.data.actualData) &&

                        }
                        TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name].showPopCallback()
                      });
                    } else {
                      if (!(TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name] && config.data.actualData[0].status === 1)) {
                        return fn._docReady(true);
                      }
                      TimesApps.PopUpList[config.data.actualData[0].name].showPopCallback()
                    }

        _saveAndMakeReady(data, pageViews) {
          if(data?.actualData &&
            Array.isArray(data?.actualData) &&
            data.actualData.length > 0 && pageViews && pageViews > 0){
            // eslint-disable-next-line guard-for-in, no-restricted-syntax
            data.actualData.some((singleData, index) => {
                if (singleData.status === 1) {
                    const shouldRepeat = singleData.forceRepeat || singleData.repeat;
                    if (shouldRepeat) {
                        singleData.priority = data.actualData[data.actualData.length - 1].priority + 1;
                        singleData.status = 0;
                        data.actualData.push(singleData);
                    }
                    data.actualData.shift();
                }
                if(data.actualData && Array.isArray(data.actualData) && data.actualData.length > 0){
                  singleData = data.actualData[0];
                  if (data.nextPageView === pageViews) {
                      singleData.status = 1;
                      data.nextPageView = pageViews + data.burninterval + 1;
                      return true;
                  }
                }
            });
            localStorage.setItem(config.browserStorageKey, JSON.stringify(data));
          }
        },
        _registerPopUp(id, callBack) {
          let callbacks = {};
          try{
            const popUp = fn._createPopUpObject(id, callBack);
            if (!popUp) return null;
            callbacks = {
              onReadyCallback: fn._onReadyCallback.bind(popUp),
              onShowCallback: fn._onShowCallback.bind(popUp),
              onUserActionCallback: popUp.onUserActionCallback,
              getDetail: fn._getDetails.bind(popUp),
            };
            popUp.callbacks = callbacks;
            TimesApps.PopUpList[id] = popUp;
            let data = JSON.parse(
              localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey),
            );
            let actualData = Array.isArray(data.actualData) && data.actualData.length > 0 ? data.actualData.map((d)=> d.name).sort() : [];
            let popupList = Object.keys(TimesApps.PopUpList).sort();
            if (actualData.join() === popupList.join()){
              document.dispatchEvent(TimesApps.popupManagerFullyInitilizedEvent);
            }
          } catch (err) {}
          return callbacks;
        },
        _getDetails(){
            return this.getDetailsPopUp();
        },
        _onReadyCallback(status) {
          this.onReadyCallback(status);
        },
        _onShowCallback(status) {
            /*
             * popup displayed
             */
            debugLogs('*** onShowCallback', this, status);
            this.onShowCallback(status);
            fn._setStatusInStorage(this, status);
          },
          _setStatusInStorage(obj, status) {
            const data = fn._getStatusFromStorage();
            const index = fn._getIndex(data.actualData, obj.id);
            data.actualData[index].lastShownTimeStamp = Date.now();
            data.actualData[index].shown = status;
            data.actualData[index].atPageView = parseInt(
                localStorage.getItem('pageViewsAfterGDPR'),
                10,
            )
            if( data?.actualData && Array.isArray(data?.actualData) && data?.actualData.length){
              data.actualData.shift();
              fn._setStatusFromStorage(data);
            }
            if (status === false) {
              fn._docReady(true);
            }
          },
          _getIndex(data, named) {
            let index = -1;
            if(data){
                Object.keys(data).forEach((key, i) => {
                    if (data[key].name === named) {
                        index = i;
                    }
                });
            }
            return index;
          },
        _createPopUpObject(id, showCallback = null) {
            const popUpdata = {};
            const data = fn._getStatusFromStorage();
            if (!(data && data.actualData)){
                return null;
            }
            const { priority, lastShownTimeStamp, name } = data.actualData.find(
              item => item.name === id,
            ) || {};
            if (name){
              popUpdata.lastShownTimeStamp = lastShownTimeStamp;
              return new TimesApps.PopupV2(name, showCallback, priority, popUpdata);
            }
        },
        _isPopuManagerRunningInSession() {
          if (localStorage.getItem("pageViewsAfterGDPR") && fn._getStatusFromStorage()) return true;
          return false;
        },
        _setStatusFromStorage(data) {
            localStorage.setItem(config.browserStorageKey, JSON.stringify(data));
        },
        _getStatusFromStorage() {
          const jsonData = localStorage.getItem(config.browserStorageKey);
          let data;
  
          try {
            data = JSON.parse(jsonData) || {};
          } catch (e) {
            data = null;
            //console.log('popupManager, JSON error');
          }

          return data;
        },
      };

      fn._docReady();
      const regiteredPopup = window.TimesApps.PopUpV2Manager.cmd || [];
      setTimeout(()=>{
        fn._init();
      },100)

      const api = {

                if(typeof callback === 'function'){

                }
            }

        },

          return fn._docReady(forcefully);
        },
      };

      return api;
    })();

          (window.pbjs && typeof window.pbjs.requestBids === 'function') ||
          (window.PWT && typeof window.PWT.requestBids === 'function')

    window.DisplayBlkrDetected = function(type) {
      window._dfpObj.displayBlkrEnabled = window._dfpObj.getCookie('displayRender')
        ? window._dfpObj.getCookie('displayRender')
        : null;
      if (type === 'prebidBlocked') window._dfpObj.displayBlkrEnabled = 0;
      if (
        (parseInt(window._dfpObj.displayBlkrEnabled) === 0 ||
          window.prebidBlocked) &&
        !window._dfpObj.displayShieldExecuted
